			<div id="sp-testimonial-free-wrapper-71345" class="sp-testimonial-free-wrapper"><div id="sp-testimonial-free-71345" class="sp-testimonial-free-section tfree-style-theme-one-v2" dir="ltr" data-preloader="" data-swiper='{&quot;dots&quot;: 1,&quot;pagination_type&quot;: &quot;dots&quot;, &quot;spaceBetween&quot;: 20, &quot;adaptiveHeight&quot;: false, &quot;pauseOnHover&quot;: true, &quot;slidesToShow&quot;: 3, &quot;speed&quot;: 600, &quot;arrows&quot;: &quot;1&quot;, &quot;autoplay&quot;: true, &quot;autoplaySpeed&quot;: 3000, &quot;swipe&quot;: true, &quot;swipeToSlide&quot;: false, &quot;draggable&quot;: true, &quot;freeMode&quot;: false, &quot;rtl&quot;: false, &quot;infinite&quot;: true,&quot;slidesPerView&quot;: {&quot;lg_desktop&quot;:3 , &quot;desktop&quot;: 3, &quot;laptop&quot;:2 , &quot;tablet&quot;: 1, &quot;mobile&quot;: 1},&quot;navigation_mobile&quot;: true, &quot;pagination_mobile&quot;:true, &quot;autoplay_mobile&quot;:true}' ><div class="swiper-wrapper"><div class="sp-testimonial-item swiper-slide"><div class="sp-testimonial-free"><div class="sp-testimonial-details"><div class="sp-testimonial-title"><h3 class="sp-testimonial-post-title">Fatima Zahoor</h3></div><div class="sp-testimonial-client-testimonial"><div class="sp-testimonial-content"><p>I recommend TechX Pakistan to all my students studying media and communication. It&#8217;s a perfect example of modern digital journalism &#8211; timely, accurate, and engaging. Their educational content about scholarships and university updates is incredibly helpful. The platform has grown tremendously since 2019, and their commitment to quality hasn&#8217;t wavered. Proud to have such a professional media outlet representing Pakistan!</p></div></div><h4 class="sp-testimonial-client-name">Fatima Zahoor</h4><div class="sp-testimonial-client-rating"><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i></div> <div class="sp-testimonial-client-designation">University Lecturer, Peshawar</div></div></div> </div> <div class="sp-testimonial-item swiper-slide"><div class="sp-testimonial-free"><div class="sp-testimonial-details"><div class="sp-testimonial-title"><h3 class="sp-testimonial-post-title">Kamran Javed</h3></div><div class="sp-testimonial-client-testimonial"><div class="sp-testimonial-content"><p>TechX Pakistan has transformed how I consume news. Instead of jumping between multiple websites, I get everything in one place &#8211; economy, finance, auto industry, real estate, and technology. Their analysis of Pakistan&#8217;s economic policies and business environment is thorough and unbiased. The tax calculator tool has saved me hours of work. This is journalism done right!</p></div></div><h4 class="sp-testimonial-client-name">Kamran Javed </h4><div class="sp-testimonial-client-rating"><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i></div> <div class="sp-testimonial-client-designation">Business Analyst, Multan</div></div></div> </div> <div class="sp-testimonial-item swiper-slide"><div class="sp-testimonial-free"><div class="sp-testimonial-details"><div class="sp-testimonial-title"><h3 class="sp-testimonial-post-title">Zainab Nasir</h3></div><div class="sp-testimonial-client-testimonial"><div class="sp-testimonial-content"><p>As a designer working with international clients, I need to stay updated on global design trends and local tech news.
